***айда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:айда.html>айда́</a> (17338)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Supposedly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">әйдә</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">äydä</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Possibly related to hajde.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:айда.html>айда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ajdá</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> let's go, c'mon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:айда.html>айда́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дома́м</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Xvátit rabótatʹ, <b>ajdá</b> po domám</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Enough of the work, let's go home.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:айда.html>айда́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:футбол.html>футбо́л</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ajdá</b> v futból.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Let's play football.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> made off; dashed away; vanished
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поругаться.html>поруга́лись</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собрать.html>собра́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вещичка.html>вещи́чки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:айда.html>айда́</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My porugálisʹ, on sobrál veščíčki i <b>ajdá</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We had a quarrel, then he got his belongings and left.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:айда.html>Айда́</a></b> is used mostly as an imperative verb, but it is invariable. In Russian grammar <b><a href = vnd.unilang:айда.html>айда́</a></b> does not count as a true verb and is considered to be closer to an interjection (<a href = vnd.unilang:междометие.html>междоме́тие</a>).
</p>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ай.html>ай</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да́</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:междометие.html>Междоме́тие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> предикатив; неизменяемое.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-айда-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ка<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ми.html>ми</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-академиj-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-я</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аккомпанировавший.html>аккомпани́ровавший</a> (28295)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккомпанировавший.html>аккомпани́ровавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akkompanírovavšij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аккомпанировать.html>аккомпани́ровать</a> (28295)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккомпанировать.html>аккомпани́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akkompanírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">саккомпани́ровать</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проаккомпани́ровать</b>)

***аккредитовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аккредитовать.html>аккредитова́ть</a> (30126)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">akredytować</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">accréditer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккредитовать.html>аккредитова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akkreditovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to accredit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to send with letters credential, as an ambassador, envoy, or diplomatic agent; to authorize, as a messenger or delegate.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">аккредита́ция</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">akkreditácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ак<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>кре<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ди.html>ди</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, двувидовой (<a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образовывать.html>образо́вывать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 2a.
<a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>До</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:середина.html>середи́ны</a> 1930-х <a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:написание.html>написа́ния</a>: <i>акредитовать</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́й</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a>»).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-аккредит-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ова</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратно.html>аккура́тно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akkurátno</span>)

</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратный.html>аккура́тный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">akkurátnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратность.html>аккура́тность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akkurátnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратность.html>аккура́тности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратность.html>аккура́тности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратность.html>аккура́тностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tidiness, neatness</li>
<li>exactness, accuracy</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратный.html>аккура́тный</a> (4757)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">accūrātus</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аккуратный.html>аккура́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">akkurátnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)аккура́тнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)аккура́тней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>accurate, punctual, exact, thorough</li>
<li>tidy, neat</li>
<li>careful, cautious</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***актив.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:актив.html>акти́в</a> (9723)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:актив.html>акти́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">aktív</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:актив.html>акти́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:актив.html>акти́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:актив.html>акти́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>group of activists, active members or leading players</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finance</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> asset</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> successes, achievements</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:активизироваться.html>активизи́ровавшийся</a> (28245)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
